# Modules

## binding (Device ID)

## TrueId

## Mouse

## Clean KeyStroke

## IP (Location) (WebRTC => google web sever) (MaxMind DB in backend) // Enrich location from backend

## Screen

## Fonts

## TeamViwer

## SkipToContent

## Clipboard (Copy & Paste)

## Headers (Live with it) (User Agent)

## VisibilityHidden
